      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n22221-5" target="شَرْكَةٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n22224"/></foreign>, (MF, TA,) and so is   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n22221-6" target="شُرْكَةٌ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n22225"/></foreign>, with damm, (K,) this last said by MF to be unknown, but it is common in Syria, almost to the exclusion of the other dial. vars. mentioned above. (TA.) An ex. of the first occurs in a trad, of Mo'ádh, <foreign lang="ar">أَجَازَ بَيْنَ أَهْلِ اليَمَنِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الشِّرْكَ</foreign>, meaning [<hi rend="ital">He allowed, among the people of El-Yemen,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">the sharing, one with another,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">الاِشْتِرَاك</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">in land</hi> [and app. <hi rend="ital">its produce</hi>], <hi rend="ital">by its owner giving it to another for the half</hi> [app. <hi rend="ital">of its produce</hi>], or <hi rend="ital">the third,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like thereof:</hi> and a similar ex. of the same word occurs in another trad. (TA.) See also an ex. in a verse cited above, conj. 3. And one says, <foreign lang="ar">رَغِبْنَا فِى شِرْكِكُمْ</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">We are desirous of sharing with you in affinity,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">relationship by marriage.</hi> (K, * TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <hi rend="ital">A share:</hi> (Mgh, O, Msb, TA:) as in the saying, <foreign lang="ar">بِيعَ شِرْكٌ مِنْ دَارِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">A share of his house was sold</hi>]: (Mgh:) and as in the saying, <foreign lang="ar">أَعْتَقَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">شِرْكًا لَهُ فِى عَبْدٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He emancipated a share belonging to him in a slave</hi>]: (Msb:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَشْرَاكٌ</foreign>. (O, Msb, TA.) [See a verse of Lebeed cited voce <foreign lang="ar">زَعَامَةٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  It is also a subst. from <foreign lang="ar">أَشْرَكَ بِٱللّٰهِ</foreign>; (Mgh, Msb, K, TA;) thus in the Kur xxxi. 12; (Mgh, TA;) meaning The <hi rend="ital">attribution of a</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">شَرِيك</foreign> [or <hi rend="ital">copartner</hi> &amp;c., or <hi rend="ital">of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">شُرَكَآء</foreign> i. e. <hi rend="ital">copartners</hi> &amp;c., (see 4,)] <hi rend="ital">to God:</hi> (Mgh:) [so that it may be rendered <hi rend="ital">belief in a plurality of gods:</hi>] and [in a wider sense,] <hi rend="ital">unbelief</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">misbelief</hi>]; syn. <foreign lang="ar">كُفْرٌ</foreign>. (S, Msb, K, TA.) And it is also expl. as meaning <hi rend="ital">Hypocrisy:</hi> (Mgh, TA:) so in the saying of the Prophet, <foreign lang="ar">إِنَّ أَخْوَفَ مَا أَخَافُ عَلَى أُمَّتِى الشِّرْكُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Verily the most fearful of what I fear for my people is hypocrisy</hi>]: (Mgh:) and so in the trad., <foreign lang="ar">الشِّرْكُ أَخْفَى فِى أُمَّتِى مِنْ دَبِيبِ النَّمْلِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Hypocrisy is more latent in my people than the creeping of ants</hi>]. (IAth, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">شَرِيكٌ</foreign>, in two places.
